neighbors on the block took a vote I am quitin base or else They want us to move

 before long, we were seizing 60 kilos of base a day We thought we were making a huge difference

suit up against a new enemy base that is menacing our society
So no to base because it is killing our children and threatening our values
when it comes to base and alcohol  just say no
I do not smuggle base
